no longer existing object
Wikidata claims that this object no longer exists. Historical, no longer existing object should not be mapped in OSM (except temporary marking to avoid remapping them from aerial imagery or similar sources) - so it means that either Wikidata is mistaken or has only partial data - for example it is fine to link ruins of a church to its wikipedia entry ( see https://www.wikidata.org/w/index.php?title=Wikidata:Project_chat&oldid=1361617968#Tagging_ruins/remains_left_after_object ) or wikipedia/wikidata tag is wrong or OSM has an outdated object that should be removed. REMEMBER TO VERIFY! WIKIDATA QUALITY MAY BE POOR!
